*** Converter from CSV table to Vec/Map format
CSV tables as read in by ~clojure.data.csv/read-csv~ are in a format vector-of-vectors matrix format. This allows fast access, but isn't convenient to use b/c you must track which column corresponds to which variable. It also doesn't compose as well in Clojure. I convert instead to a vector-of-maps format, where the map's keys are the column names. To get a column one simply does ~(map :keyword data)~ instead of ~(map #(get % column-number) data)~
#+BEGIN_SRC clojure :exports code
  (defn csv-2-map
    "Takes a CSV (as coming from `clojure.data.csv`) and turn it into Vec a Map's.
    With Map keys being the column names
    Key names are cleaned to not have spaces. Spaces are replaces with `-` "
    [csv]
    (let [header (->> (nth csv 0)
		      (map #(clojure.string/replace % #"[() ]" "-"))
		      (map keyword))]
    
      (->> (rest csv)
	   (mapv #(zipmap header %)))))
#+END_SRC

#+RESULTS:
: #'user/csv-2-map

#+BEGIN_SRC clojure :exports code
(defn svg-to-org
  "This takes the SVG hiccup, serializes and inserts new line characters
  If the SVG is one long line, then Emacs is not happy"
  [svg]
  (-> svg
       serialize
       (clojure.string/replace #"><" ">\n<")))

  (defn mm-plot
    [data
     start-date
     width
     height
     left-margin]
      (-> {:x-axis (linear-axis
		    {:domain [0 366]
		     :range  [left-margin width]
		     :minor  30
		     :label-style {:fill "none"}
		     :pos    height})
	   :y-axis (-> (linear-axis {:domain  [0 300]
		                     :range   [height 0]
		                     :major  100
		                     :minor  10
		                     :pos    left-margin})
                       (assoc :major [100]))
                       
	   :grid {:minor-x true
		  :minor-y false}
	   :data [{:values  (->> data
				 (mapv #(vector (->> %
						     :Date
						     tick/date
						     (tick/new-interval start-date)
						     tick/duration
						     tick/days)
						(-> %
						    :Rain--mm-
						    read-string))))
		   :attribs {:fill "none" :stroke "red"}
		   :layout  svg-bar-plot}]}
	  (svg-plot2d-cartesian)))

  (defn d18O-plot
    [data
     start-date
     width
     height
     left-margin]
      (-> {:x-axis (linear-axis
		    {:domain [0 366]
		     :range  [left-margin width]
		     :minor  30
		     :label-style {:fill "none"}
		     :pos    100})
	   :y-axis (assoc (linear-axis
			   {:domain  [0 -25] ;; the first values in effect sets the bar's `zero`
			    :range   [  
				      (/  height
					  2.0)
				      height]
			    :pos    left-margin})
			  :major
			  [0 -10 -20])
	   :grid {:minor-x true
		  :minor-y false}
	   :data [{:values  (->> data
				 (mapv #(vector (->> %
						     :Date
						     tick/date
						     (tick/new-interval start-date)
						     tick/duration
						     tick/days)
						(-> %
						    :d18O
						    read-string))))
		   :attribs {:fill "none" :stroke "#0af"}
		   :layout  svg-bar-plot}]}
	  (svg-plot2d-cartesian)))

  (defn group-by-consecutive-days
    [data]
    (->> (reduce (fn [{:keys [previous-date grouped-data]}
		      new-data]
		   {:previous-date (:Date new-data)
		    :grouped-data (if (= 2 ;; start of one day to end of following day is 48H
					 (->> new-data
					      :Date
					      tick/date
					      (tick/new-interval previous-date)
					      tick/duration
					      tick/days))
				    (update grouped-data
					    0
					    #(clojure.core/into % [new-data]))
				    (clojure.core/into [[new-data]] grouped-data))})
		 {:previous-date (-> data
				     first
				     :Date
				     tick/date
				     tick/dec)
		  :grouped-data [[]]}
		 data)
	 :grouped-data
	 (filterv #(not= 1
			(count %)))))

  (defn grouped-data-to-intervals
    [grouped-data
     start-date]
    (mapv #(vector (->> %
		       first
		       :Date
		       tick/date
		       (tick/new-interval start-date)
		       tick/duration
		       tick/days)
		  (->> %
		       last
		       :Date
		       tick/date
		       (tick/new-interval start-date)
		       tick/duration
		       tick/days))
	 grouped-data))

  (defn event-interval-plot
    [data
     start-date
     width
     height
     left-margin]
    (let [grouped-data (group-by-consecutive-days data)
	  intervals-in-days (grouped-data-to-intervals grouped-data
						       start-date)]
      (->> {:x-axis (linear-axis
		    {:domain [0 366]
		     :range  [left-margin width]
		     :minor  30
		     :label-style {:fill "none"}
		     :pos    height
		     :visible false})
	   :y-axis (linear-axis
		    {:domain  [0 300]
		     :range   [(* height 0.95) 0]
		     :major  100
		     :minor  10
		     :pos    left-margin
		     :visible false})
	    :data   [{:values  intervals-in-days
		      :attribs {:stroke-width "10px" :stroke-linecap "none" :stroke "grey"}
		      :layout  svg-stacked-interval-plot}]}
	   (svg-plot2d-cartesian))))

  (defn event-weighted-averages
    [grouped-data]
    (mapv (fn [event-data]
	   (let [[sum total-mm] (reduce (fn [[sum total-mm] rainy-day]
					  (let [day-mm (-> rainy-day
							   :Rain--mm-
							   read-string)
						day-d18O (-> rainy-day
							     :d18O
							     read-string)]

					    [(+ sum
						(* day-mm
						   day-d18O))
					     (+ total-mm
						day-mm)]))
					[0 0]
					event-data)
		 weighted-average (/ sum total-mm)]
	     weighted-average))
	 grouped-data))

  (defn event-average-plot
    [data
     start-date
     width
     height
     left-margin]
    (let [grouped-data (group-by-consecutive-days data)
	  intervals-in-days (grouped-data-to-intervals grouped-data
						       start-date)
	  weighted-averages (event-weighted-averages grouped-data)
	  line-segments (mapv (fn [[segment-start-date
				    segment-end-date]
				   weighted-average]
				(println "event!: " segment-start-date " " segment-end-date " " weighted-average)
				{:layout svg-area-plot
				 :attribs {:fill "#cadbd6"}
				 :values [[segment-start-date
					   (if (neg? weighted-average)
					     weighted-average
					     0.0)]
					  [segment-end-date
					   (if (neg? weighted-average)
					     weighted-average
					     0.0)]]})
			      intervals-in-days
			      weighted-averages)]
      #_(println line-segments)
      (-> {:x-axis (linear-axis
		    {:domain [0 366]
		     :range  [left-margin width]
		     :minor  30
		     :label-style {:fill "none"}
		     :pos    100})
	   :y-axis (assoc (linear-axis
			   {:domain  [0 -25] ;; the first values in effect sets the bar's `zero`
			    :range   [  
				      (/  height
					  2.0)
				      height]
			    :pos    left-margin})
			  :major
			  [0 -10 -20])
	   :grid {:minor-x true
		  :minor-y false}
	   :data #_[{:values [[0 -10][10 -10]]
		     :attribs {:fill "none" :stroke "#0af"}
		     :layout svg-area-plot}]
	   line-segments #_[{:values  (->> data
					   (mapv #(vector (->> %
							       :Date
							       tick/date
							       (tick/new-interval start-date)
							       tick/duration
							       tick/days)
							  (-> %
							      :d18O
							      read-string))))
			     :attribs {:fill "none" :stroke "#0af"}
			     :layout  svg-bar-plot}]}
	  (svg-plot2d-cartesian))
      ))



  (defn combined-plot
    [start-date
     width
     height
     data]
    (let [margin-size 100
	  ;; data  (filterv #(clojure.core/< 1.0 (-> %
	  ;; 								:Rain--mm-
	  ;; 								read-string))
	  ;;                data)
	  ]
      (group {}
	     (group {}
		    (text [0 120] "d18O")
		    #_(event-average-plot (filterv #(clojure.core/< 1.0 (-> %
									  :Rain--mm-
									  read-string))
						 data)
					start-date
					width
					height
					margin-size)
		    (d18O-plot data
			       start-date
			       width
			       height
			       margin-size))
	     (group {:transform (geom/translate M32
						[0 -100])} 
		    (mm-plot data
			     start-date
			     width
			     height
			     margin-size)
		    (text [0 185] "Rain (mm)")
		    (text [(+ margin-size 5) 110] (str (->> data
							    first
							    :Date
							    tick/date
                                                            tick/year
                                                            tick/int))
                          #_(str "One Year Period. Starting on: "
						       (->> data
							    first
							    :Date
							    tick/date
							    (tick/format (tick.format/formatter "yyyy-MM-dd")))
						       " Ending on: "
						       (->> data
							    last
							    :Date
							    tick/date
							    (tick/format (tick.format/formatter "yyyy-MM-dd"))))))

	     (group {:transform (geom/translate M32
						[0 0])}
		    #_(event-interval-plot (filterv #(clojure.core/< 1.0 (-> %
									  :Rain--mm-
									  read-string))
						 data)
					 start-date
					 width
					 height
					 margin-size)

		    #_(text [0 (* height 0.975)] "Rain Events ->")))))


  (defn make-charts
    ([data
      width
      height]
     (make-charts data
		  width
		  height
		  0
		  nil))
    ([data
      width
      height
      offset
      combined-svg]
     (println offset)
     (let [start-date (-> data
			   first
			   :Date
			   tick/date
                           tick/year ;; Fix start-date to Jan 1st
                           tick/int
                           (tick/new-date 1
                                          1))
	   end-date (-> start-date
                        #_#_#_#_
                        data
			first
			:Date
			tick/date
			(tick/>> (tick/new-period 1 :years)))
	   sorted-data (clojure.core/group-by #(-> %
						   :Date
						   tick/date
						   (tick/relation end-date))
					      data)
	   rain-in-year (:precedes sorted-data)
	   svg-of-chart (->> rain-in-year
			     (combined-plot start-date
					    width
					    height)
			     #_(svg {:width width :height height}))
	   other-rains (:preceded-by sorted-data)]
       (if (nil? other-rains)
	 (svg {:width width
	       :height offset
	       :viewBox (str "0 0 "
			     (+ width
				25)
			     " "
			     offset)}
	      combined-svg)
	 (make-charts other-rains
		      width
		      height
		      (+ offset height)
		      (if (nil? combined-svg)
		       svg-of-chart
			(group {}
			       combined-svg
			       (group {:transform (geom/translate M32
								  [0 offset])}
				      svg-of-chart))))))))
#+END_SRC

Write out rain event data to a CSV:
#+BEGIN_SRC clojure
    (defn rain-event-stats
      [rain-event]
      (let [[total-rain-during-event-mm
	     weighted-sum-d18O]  (reduce (fn [[total-rain-mm
					       weighted-sum-d18O]
					      rainy-day]
					   #_(println rainy-day)
					   (let [rain-mm (-> rainy-day
							     :Rain--mm-
							     read-string)
						 d18O (-> rainy-day
							  :d18O
							  read-string)]
					     [(+ total-rain-mm
						 rain-mm)
					      (+ weighted-sum-d18O
						 (* d18O
						    rain-mm))]))
					 [0 0]
					 rain-event)
	    weighted-average-d18O (/ weighted-sum-d18O
				     total-rain-during-event-mm)]
	{:start-date (-> rain-event
			 first
			 :Date)
	 :end-data (-> rain-event
		       last
		       :Date)
	 :total-rain-mm total-rain-during-event-mm
	 :weighted-average-d18O weighted-average-d18O}))


    (let [filtered-data (filterv #(clojure.core/< 1.0 (-> %
							  :Rain--mm-
							  read-string))
				 rain-data)
	  grouped-data (group-by-consecutive-days filtered-data)
	  ;; intervals-in-days (grouped-data-to-intervals grouped-data
	  ;;   					   (->> rain-data
	  ;;   						first
	  ;;   						:Date
	  ;;   						tick/date))
	  event-info (map rain-event-stats
			  grouped-data)
	  event-info-csv-vec (mapv (fn [event]
				     (vector (:start-date event)
					     (:end-data event)
					     (:total-rain-mm event)
					     (:weighted-average-d18O event)))
				   event-info)]
      (with-open [writer (writer "event-stats.csv")]
	(write-csv writer
		   (into [["state-date" "end-date" "total-precipitation-mm" "average-d18O"]]
			 event-info-csv-vec))))
#+END_SRC
